Welcome to Optery's Open-Source Data Broker Directory, the largest and most comprehensive resource of structured data on data brokers and opting out.

This directory features detailed profiles for more than 956 data brokers, including direct opt-out links and step-by-step opt-out guides.

It is continuously updated and provided free to the public to increase transparency and help individuals take control of their personal data.

Individuals can use [Optery's free exposure scan](https://app.optery.com/signup) to identify which of the data brokers in this directory are currently publishing their personal information on the web.

Unlike other data broker scanning tools, Optery’s patented technology generates a personalized exposure report containing live screenshots and links to the results.

We hope this directory helps increase visibility into the data-broker ecosystem and supports individuals’ ongoing efforts to strengthen their privacy and security.

## **Using This Directory**

### **Data Formats**

The directory is available in multiple formats for different use cases:

* JSON (data/data-brokers.json) — best for programmatic access, APIs, and data analysis  
* CSV (data/data-brokers.csv) — best for Excel, Google Sheets, or database imports  
* Markdown (data/data-brokers.md) — best for browsing on GitHub

### **What's Included**

Each data-broker entry includes (when available):

* Broker name and website  
* Direct opt-out URLs  
* Links to written and video opt-out guides  
* Contact information (email, website)  
* Broker type classification  
* Optery support tier  
* Description of the broker

Note: Some entries may not have complete information for all fields.

## **Use Cases**

This dataset is valuable for:

* Privacy researchers – analyzing data-broker practices and industry trends  
* Journalists – investigating the data-broker industry  
* Educators – teaching about data privacy and digital rights  
* Individuals – locating data brokers and beginning manual opt-outs  
* Developers – incorporating data broker data sets and opt out details in their applications

## **Updates**

The directory is maintained and regularly updated by Optery with new data brokers, verified contact details, and opt-out procedures.

You can watch this repository for updates or use the searchable directory version on our website at [optery.com/data-brokers](https://www.optery.com/data-brokers).

## **License**

This directory is licensed under CC BY-NC-SA 4.0. You may share and adapt this material for noncommercial purposes with attribution. For commercial use, contact support@optery.com.

## **About Optery**

Optery helps individuals and organizations reduce the risks of physical and cyberattacks by identifying and removing personal information from hundreds of data brokers and people-search sites. Optery was ranked the \#1 most effective of all personal data removal services tested in a 2024 study by Consumer Reports, and is the most-awarded personal data-removal service in the industry: PCMag Editors’ Choice (2022–2025), Cyber Defense Magazine Top InfoSec Innovator (2024–2025), SiliconANGLE TechForward Award (2025), Fortress Cybersecurity Award (2025), Cybersecurity Excellence Awards (2024–2025), and Fast Company’s Next Big Things in Tech (2023). Learn more at optery.com.

## Data Broker Details

<a id='26729'></a>
## 1called.com

### Description
1called.com operates as a global reverse phone number lookup service, enabling users to identify the source of unknown calls. By entering a phone number into its search bar, individuals can potentially access information linked to that number, such as the owner's name and location. The service claims to have information on all phone numbers worldwide, allowing for anonymous searches without requiring registration. This easy access to personal data creates considerable privacy concerns, as it can be exploited for doxxing, stalking, harassment, and fraud. Malicious actors could use the service to connect a phone number to an individual's identity and location, increasing their vulnerability. To protect their privacy, individuals should limit the public sharing of their personal phone numbers and actively seek to remove their information from such online directories.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://www.1called.com/](https://www.1called.com/)
- **Type**: Phone Directory
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

---

<a id='27231'></a>
## 1who.net

### Description
1who.net is a free and simple reverse phone number lookup service that allows users to identify the owner of a phone number. The website provides a search bar where anyone can enter a phone number to access associated information, which may include the owner's name and address. While the full scope of its database is not public, such services typically aggregate data from public records and other sources. The primary users are individuals curious about an unknown caller. The public availability of this information poses significant privacy risks, as it can be exploited for doxxing, stalking, harassment, and identity theft. Malicious actors could use this data to link a phone number to a physical address and other personal details, increasing a person's vulnerability. To protect their privacy, individuals should be cautious about sharing their phone number online and can request to have their information removed from such databases.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://1who.net](https://1who.net)
- **Type**: Phone Directory
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

---

<a id='17289'></a>
## 411.com

### Description
411.com is a people search directory. Anyone can search using a name, phone number or address to reveal a person’s current and past home addresses, age, names of relatives, and other public records. Sites like 411.com often sell personal information to third-party advertisers and companies for marketing purposes – without the consent or knowledge of the individuals.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://www.411.com/](https://www.411.com/)
- **Opt-Out URL**: [https://www.whitepages.com/suppression-requests](https://www.whitepages.com/suppression-requests)
- **Opt-Out Guide**: [https://www.optery.com/411-com-how-to-opt-out-of-411-com-step-by-step-instructions/](https://www.optery.com/411-com-how-to-opt-out-of-411-com-step-by-step-instructions/)
- **Opt-Out Video Guide**: [https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=scIwia0-y0k](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=scIwia0-y0k)
- **Email**: support@whitepages.com
- **Type**: People Search Site
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Ultimate](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

---

<a id='18611'></a>
## 411.info

### Description
411.info is the first online 411 service in US and Canada. Offering a free online information service, this data broker aims to help individuals locate people, businesses, services, and addresses. Moreover, the online services they offer are free of charge, in contrast to telephone-based 411 services. The online directory services offered on their website make it easy to connect with people and services, but this also means it leaves us exposed online. Our valuable personal and business information is bought and shared online in just a few clicks without our knowledge. This often results in phishing attempts, and unwanted spam calls and emails. If you are concerned about your personal or company online security, we have created Step-by-Step instructions on How to Opt Out of 411.info-Business below.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://411.info](https://411.info)
- **Opt-Out URL**: [https://411.info/manage/](https://411.info/manage/)
- **Opt-Out Guide**: [https://www.optery.com/411-info-how-to-opt-out-of-411-info-step-by-step-instructions/](https://www.optery.com/411-info-how-to-opt-out-of-411-info-step-by-step-instructions/)
- **Email**: privacy@411.info
- **Type**: People Search Site
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Ultimate](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

---

<a id='26335'></a>
## 411reverselookup.ca

### Description
411reverselookup.ca is a Canadian online reverse phone number lookup service. Powered by the Canada411 and Yellow Pages databases, it allows users to identify the owner of a residential or business phone number in Canada. Users can enter a full 10-digit phone number to find a specific listing or a 7-digit number to see all listings containing that sequence. If a number is not in their database, the service may still provide general information such as the city and province of origin, the carrier, and whether it is a cell number or landline. The public availability of this information can be exploited by malicious actors for phishing scams, unsolicited marketing calls, or to gather personal details for doxxing and harassment. This exposure of personal contact information, even when limited, contributes to a higher risk of individuals being targeted for various forms of fraud. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about where they share their phone number online and can request to have their information removed from such directories.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://www.411reverselookup.ca/](https://www.411reverselookup.ca/)
- **Type**: Phone Directory
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

---

<a id='26426'></a>
## 6sense Insights, Inc.

### Description
6sense is a revenue intelligence platform that utilizes artificial intelligence to support business-to-business (B2B) marketing and sales teams. The service captures and analyzes vast amounts of online data, referred to as "buying signals," to predict which companies are actively looking to purchase specific products or services. Its primary customers are enterprise sales and marketing departments in sectors like technology, finance, and manufacturing, who use the platform to identify and prioritize high-value accounts for their outreach campaigns. While 6sense focuses on business data, it collects and provides professional contact information, including names, job titles, and corporate email addresses, to its subscribers. This practice poses a risk to professional privacy, as it can lead to an increase in unsolicited marketing emails and sales calls. To mitigate this, individuals should be mindful of the professional information they share online and can request to have their data removed by submitting an opt-out request through the 6sense privacy center.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://6sense.com/](https://6sense.com/)
- **Opt-Out URL**: [https://6sense.com/privacy-policy/](https://6sense.com/privacy-policy/)
- **Email**: privacy@6sense.com
- **Type**: B2B Lead Generation
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

---

<a id='26670'></a>
## AMF Internet Services Limited

### Description
Anymail Finder, operated by AMF Internet Services Limited, is a tool designed to find professional email addresses for individuals at specific companies. Its primary customers include sales, marketing, and human resources professionals who use the service for lead generation, outreach, and recruitment. The platform scrapes public web sources and uses direct server validation to discover and verify corporate email patterns, a key feature being that users are only charged for emails that are successfully verified. By making business contact information readily available, the service exposes individuals to a higher risk of unsolicited marketing emails, spam, and targeted phishing scams by malicious actors. These risks are heightened as the service allows for bulk searching, enabling large-scale data collection for outreach campaigns. To mitigate this exposure, individuals should be cautious about where their professional contact information is shared online and can request to have their information removed from the platform's database via an opt-out process.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://anymailfinder.com/](https://anymailfinder.com/)
- **Opt-Out URL**: [https://anymailfinder.com/legal/gdpr](https://anymailfinder.com/legal/gdpr)
- **Email**: legal@anymailfinder.com
- **Type**: B2B Lead Generation
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

<a id='26463'></a>
## AddrHistory

### Description
AddrHistory.com provides a searchable database of property records across the United States, allowing users to find information by address or homeowner name. The site claims to have over 18 million property records, 30 million sale records, and 164 million tax records from thousands of cities. This service exposes personal information by linking individuals to their current and past addresses, alongside property sales and tax history, which could be used by anyone for various purposes. The accessibility of this data poses significant privacy risks, including doxxing, stalking, and providing bad actors with information that could be used for harassment or to piece together even more detailed personal profiles. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about the information they share publicly and can request to have their records removed from such databases.

### Information

<a id='26434'></a>
## Amedisys, Inc.

### Description
Amedisys, Inc. is a prominent American healthcare company that provides home health, hospice, and palliative care services. Rather than operating as a public data broker, Amedisys functions as a healthcare provider, creating detailed patient profiles to deliver personalized medical care and support in patients' homes. Their services are primarily for individuals recovering from illness or surgery, or managing long-term conditions, and are coordinated with physicians and hospitals across the United States. The company collects and manages extensive personal and highly sensitive protected health information (PHI), which is governed by the Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act (HIPAA). The primary privacy risk associated with Amedisys is not the public sale or exposure of data, but the potential for a data breach, which could expose extremely sensitive medical histories and personal identifiers. Such a breach could lead to medical identity theft, targeted fraud, and discrimination. Because Amedisys does not sell patient information, the risks of stalking or general harassment from public data exposure are minimal. Individuals under their care can best protect themselves by understanding their rights under HIPAA, reviewing the company's privacy notices, and being cautious about sharing their health information.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://www.amedisys.com/](https://www.amedisys.com/)
- **Opt-Out URL**: [https://cdn.amedisys.com/userfiles/CCPA%20Request%20Form.pdf](https://cdn.amedisys.com/userfiles/CCPA%20Request%20Form.pdf)

## Ancestry.com UK Limited

### Description
Ancestry.co.uk is the UK-specific platform of the global genealogy giant, Ancestry, which provides access to billions of historical records to help users research and construct their family trees. The service is primarily used by individuals interested in discovering their family history and building a comprehensive picture of their lineage. Beyond record collections, a significant and popular feature is its DNA testing service, which offers insights into a user's ethnic origins and connects them with potential relatives within the vast Ancestry DNA network. The immense database of personal information, including names, birth dates, family relationships, and sensitive genetic data, raises considerable privacy concerns. This concentration of personal and familial data could be a target for bad actors, potentially leading to risks of identity theft, fraud, and social engineering. To safeguard their information, individuals should be cautious about the extent of personal data they share publicly on the platform and utilize the available privacy settings to control the visibility of their family tree and DNA information. Users also have the option to request the deletion of their data and account.

### Information

<a id='27235'></a>
## Background Alert, Inc.

### Description
Background Alert, Inc. operated as a people search website that provided detailed reports on individuals by aggregating billions of public records. The service allowed users to find information such as full names, current and past addresses, age, birth and death records, criminal records, and marriage and divorce history. By compiling and selling these comprehensive profiles, the platform exposed sensitive personal data that could be exploited for identity theft, stalking, doxxing, and harassment. The company's practices were notable as they not only provided public data but also drew inferences to identify potential associates of an individual, creating further privacy risks. In early 2025, Background Alert, Inc. agreed to cease operations for three years as part of a settlement with the California Privacy Protection Agency for failing to register as a data broker. To protect oneself from the exposure of personal data, individuals should be cautious about the information they share online and can request data removal from active data broker sites.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://backgroundalert.com](https://backgroundalert.com)
- **Email**: info@BackgroundAlert.com

<a id='26436'></a>
## Brady List

### Description
Brady List operates as a specialized platform that aggregates and provides public-facing information regarding law enforcement officer misconduct. The service compiles data such as public complaints, decertification records, use-of-force reports, and other potential impeachment disclosures into profiles of individual officers across the United States. This information is intended for use in the legal field, particularly by prosecutors who are required by the *Brady* and *Giglio* legal doctrines to disclose any evidence that could impact the credibility of a law enforcement witness to the defense. The primary customers are legal professionals, including prosecutors, defense attorneys, and government organizations. The public accessibility of this sensitive information poses significant privacy and professional risks to the law enforcement officers listed. Exposure on this platform can lead to doxxing, harassment, and threats to personal safety for the officers and their families. Furthermore, being included in such a database can have severe career repercussions, potentially jeopardizing an officer's ability to testify in court and leading to termination of employment. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about the information they share publicly and can seek to have inaccurate information corrected or removed where possible, though the platform's primary function is to disclose public record information.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://giglio-bradylist.com/](https://giglio-bradylist.com/)
- **Type**: Profile Data Broker
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

<a id='26311'></a>
## CallApp Software Ltd.

### Description
CallApp is a mobile application that provides caller ID, call blocking, and call recording services to a global user base. Its primary function is to identify unknown callers, with a database reportedly containing over eight billion phone numbers. The application gathers information from public sources and its users' contact lists, enriching this data with details from social media platforms to create more comprehensive caller profiles. While its main users are individuals seeking to block spam and identify unknown numbers, CallApp also offers services for businesses to brand their outgoing calls. The collection and publication of personal phone numbers and associated names, often without the direct consent of the individuals listed, poses significant privacy risks, including potential harassment, stalking, and doxxing. Bad actors could misuse this readily available contact information to target individuals for scams or other malicious activities. To protect their information, individuals should be mindful of the permissions granted to applications and can request to have their number removed from the service's searchable database through an unlisting process on the CallApp website.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://callapp.com/](https://callapp.com/)
- **Opt-Out URL**: [https://callapp.com/support/can-i-wipe-my-information-from-callapp-2](https://callapp.com/support/can-i-wipe-my-information-from-callapp-2)
- **Email**: support@callapp.com
- **Type**: Phone Directory
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

## CallerCenter.com

### Description
CallerCenter.com is a data broker that primarily functions as a reverse phone number lookup service. It allows users to search for phone numbers and access information and public records associated with them. The platform is also a community-driven space where individuals can post comments and reports about specific phone numbers, often to identify and warn others about telemarketing, spam, or scam calls. This public exposure of phone numbers, combined with user-generated comments, poses significant privacy risks. Malicious actors could use this information for harassment or doxxing, and negative comments, even if related to a previous owner of a number, can damage an individual's reputation. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about sharing their phone number online and can request to have their information removed from such databases.

<a id='26457'></a>
## CallerIDTest

### Description
CallerIDTest.com was an online service that allowed users to perform a reverse phone number lookup to see the Caller ID Name (CNAM) associated with any U.S. or Canadian phone number. The primary use case was for businesses and individuals to verify that their own outbound caller ID information was displaying correctly, but it could also be used to identify unknown callers. The service queried the same official CNAM databases used by major telephone carriers to retrieve the name tied to a specific phone number. Although the service is now defunct due to legal challenges, its function of linking phone numbers to names posed significant privacy risks. Exposing the name connected to a phone number could facilitate doxxing, stalking, and harassment by making it easier for malicious actors to identify and target individuals. To protect against such risks, people should be cautious about where they share their phone number online and can utilize services to have their information removed from data broker databases.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://calleridtest.com/](https://calleridtest.com/)
- **Type**: Phone Directory
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

## ClustrMaps

### Description
Clustrmaps is a data broker that uses an embedded script to track visitors to a site in order to generate a heatmap. It allows users to see how many people have visited their site, where they came from, and what pages they viewed. Clustrmaps also collects public records to analyze different US cities, their social demography, and their business environment. Their records include engineering and business records, building ownership, and neighborhood profiles. Clustrmaps has also been known to sell user data to third-party companies, which raises privacy concerns. Many users are not aware of Clustrmaps and the potential privacy implications of its activities. Firstly, their website is not particularly user-friendly and can be difficult to navigate. Secondly, they track your IP address, which can be used to personally identify you. Finally, they sell access to their database of website visitors, which includes information on where you live and what pages you visit. By opting out of Clustrmaps, you can take back control of your data and protect your privacy.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://clustrmaps.com/](https://clustrmaps.com/)

<a id='26273'></a>
## Cuit Online

### Description
Cuit Online is an Argentinian web service that allows users to find an individual's or a company's CUIT (Clave Única de Identificación Tributaria), which is a unique tax identification key. The platform enables searching for this information by providing a person's DNI (Documento Nacional de Identidad), full name, or a company's name. This service is primarily used within Argentina for official and commercial transactions, as the CUIT is necessary for tax purposes for self-employed individuals, businesses, and professionals. The accessibility of this data, which links a national identifier to a tax number, poses privacy risks such as identity theft and fraud. Malicious actors could potentially use this information to impersonate individuals or businesses for financial gain or harassment. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about where they share their DNI and CUIT numbers and can request the removal of their data from such online directories.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://www.cuitonline.com/](https://www.cuitonline.com/)
- **Type**: People Search Site
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

## DATO CAPITAL LTD

### Description
Dato Capital is an international business information provider that aggregates data on companies and their directors from numerous official sources. Their database covers millions of companies and directors across various jurisdictions, including the United Kingdom, Spain, Gibraltar, Panama, and the Cayman Islands. The service is utilized by a range of clients, from individuals to large corporations and government institutions, for purposes such as due diligence, fraud investigations, and Anti-Money Laundering (AML) checks. While the platform focuses on business data, it exposes the names and corporate affiliations of company directors, making their professional history publicly searchable. This information, sourced from public records, can be used to track an individual's business network and history, posing a risk if this data is taken out of context or used for harassment. Dato Capital states that because the information is from public sources, any removal or correction requests must be handled at the original source, such as the UK's Companies House. Individuals can protect themselves by being aware of what information becomes public when they take on company director roles.

## Dateas

### Description
Dateas is an online platform that provides access to a wide variety of public records and documents from multiple countries. The service offers both free and paid options for searching and retrieving information such as genealogical records, business reports, background checks, court records, and vital records. Its primary customers include individuals researching family history, businesses seeking commercial information, and professionals in legal or administrative fields. By aggregating vast amounts of personal and professional data, Dateas makes sensitive information easily accessible, which can lead to significant privacy risks. The exposure of such detailed personal data increases the chances of identity theft, stalking, doxxing, and online harassment by malicious actors. Individuals can better protect their privacy by being cautious about the information they share online and by actively seeking to have their data removed from such databases. The platform indicates that it has a process for users to request the removal of their data.

## Dato Capital

### Description
Dato Capital is an international business information database that provides detailed information on companies and their directors across various jurisdictions, including the United Kingdom, Spain, the Netherlands, and Panama. Its primary customers are corporations, governments, and financial institutions that use the data for due diligence, fraud investigations, and anti-money laundering (AML) checks. The service compiles information from official public records, offering basic company details and selling more comprehensive reports that can include financial statements and director appointments. While the platform focuses on business data, it exposes the names of company directors and their professional affiliations, creating comprehensive profiles of their business activities. This concentration of information could be misused for targeted phishing campaigns, corporate espionage, or harassment. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about the information included in public business filings. Although Dato Capital states it generally does not remove public business information, individuals can still submit opt-out requests and should minimize their overall online data exposure.

### Description

Businesses can create a free listing on the site, which includes the business name, address, phone number, and category. Listings can also include a brief description of the business, photos, and user-generated reviews. While Dexknows does have a lot of useful information, there are some disadvantages to having your personal information on their website. One disadvantage is that your personal information may be accessed by third-party companies that DexKnows has partnered with. These companies may use your personal information for their own marketing purposes. Additionally, if you ever need to contact Dexknows customer service, you will have to provide them with your personal information. This means that your information could be shared with DexKnows employees, which could lead to identity theft in the case of a breach, hack, or leak. Optery helps you scan and remove your exposed personal information from data broker sites. ## DomainTools LLC

### Description
DomainTools is a cybersecurity company that provides detailed information about internet domains and IP addresses. Its services are primarily used by cybersecurity professionals, government agencies, and corporations for threat intelligence, fraud prevention, and brand protection. The company aggregates vast amounts of data, including historical WHOIS records, passive DNS data, and website ownership details, to help users investigate cyber threats and map out malicious infrastructure. While essential for security research, the public availability of WHOIS data, which can include names, email addresses, and phone numbers of domain registrants, poses privacy risks. This information could potentially be misused by malicious actors for doxxing, targeted phishing attacks, or harassment. To mitigate these risks, individuals can utilize domain privacy services when registering a domain to redact personal information from public WHOIS records. It is also advisable to be cautious about the personal information shared online and to be aware of how it can be accessed through services like DomainTools.

## Downing &#038; Lahey Mortuaries &#038; Crematory

### Description
Downing & Lahey Mortuaries & Crematory is a family-owned funeral home that has been serving the Wichita, Kansas area for over a century. It is not a data broker in the traditional sense, but rather provides funeral, cremation, and memorial services. The company's website features obituaries of deceased individuals, which are published with the consent of the family, and this is the extent of its "people search" functionality. While the primary business is funeral services, the online publication of obituaries does place personal information into the public domain. This information can include the deceased's name, age, date of death, and details about their life and family members. Although the risk is lower compared to typical data broker sites, this information could potentially be aggregated by malicious actors for purposes like genealogical identity theft or targeting grieving family members for scams. To protect one's privacy, it is wise to be mindful of the amount of personal information shared publicly online, even in contexts like obituaries, and to understand that this information can be requested to be removed.

<a id='26675'></a>
## Epieos

### Description
Epieos is an Open Source Intelligence (OSINT) tool that specializes in reverse email and phone number lookups to uncover an individual's digital footprint across numerous online platforms. Primarily serving professionals in cybersecurity, law enforcement, and investigative journalism, the service scans over 140 websites and social networks to link a piece of contact information to associated profiles. This allows users to aggregate publicly available data, including usernames, social media accounts, and online activities, creating a detailed personal profile from a single starting point. The exposure of this consolidated information presents significant privacy risks, as it simplifies the process for malicious actors to conduct doxxing, stalking, harassment, or identity theft by easily mapping out a person's online presence. Although Epieos states it does not log its users' searches, the data it reveals is sourced from what individuals have shared publicly. To mitigate such risks, it is crucial for individuals to minimize the personal information they share on public profiles and to actively seek removal from data broker databases.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://epieos.com/](https://epieos.com/)

- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

<a id='18630'></a>
## Epsilon

### Description
Epsilon is a data broker, which means that it collects and sells information about consumers. Epsilon’s website states that it has information on more than 200 million consumers in the United States and Canada. This information includes ”identifiable information” (i. e., name, address, phone number, email address, etc.) as well as ”identified information” (i. e., web page visits, purchase history, etc.). Epsilon also has a database of security questions that are often used to verify a person’s identity when resetting passwords or accessing account information. Read on for our step-by-step instructions on How to Opt Out of Epsilon.

### Information

Its primary purpose is to help people discover their family history by searching billions of historical documents, such as birth, marriage, and death certificates, census data, and probate records. Users can build family trees and connect with their heritage. While the platform offers invaluable data for genealogical research, the availability of personal information on deceased individuals, and potentially living individuals if incorrectly marked, could be misused for creating fraudulent identities or for social engineering schemes. The site's collaborative nature, where users can contribute to a single family tree, also introduces the risk of inaccuracies. To protect their privacy, individuals should be cautious about the information they share about living relatives and utilize the site's privacy settings to control the visibility of their personal data.

## Flexera

### Description
FlexNet Operations is a comprehensive software monetization platform from Flexera's Revenera division, designed for software vendors and intelligent device manufacturers. It is not a traditional data broker that deals with public consumer data, but rather a B2B service that enables companies to manage software licensing, entitlements, and updates for their end-users. The platform allows businesses to control and automate the fulfillment and activation of software licenses and to gain insights into how their products are being used. While it processes end-user data on behalf of its business customers, this information is related to software usage and entitlements rather than publicly sourced personal profiles. The primary risk for individuals is not public exposure of personal data, but rather how the software vendors who use FlexNet Operations collect and manage their customers' usage data. To protect their privacy, individuals should review the privacy policies of the software products they use and be mindful of the data they consent to share with software vendors.

## Foller.me

### Description
Foller.me is a free-to-use analytics tool that provides detailed insights into any public X (formerly Twitter) profile. By inputting a username, the service gathers and analyzes the user's recent tweets to generate reports on their most used topics, hashtags, and mentions. It also displays information not readily available on the platform itself, such as the account's join date, timezone, follower-to-following ratio, and the geographic location of their followers. While this data is sourced from public profiles, its aggregation and analysis can create privacy risks by allowing anyone to easily profile a user's habits, interests, and social circles, which could be exploited for targeted harassment or social engineering. The concentration of this information in one place makes it simpler for bad actors to understand a user's activity patterns. To protect their information, individuals should be mindful of what they post publicly on social media and can set their profiles to private to prevent such tools from accessing their data.

## FreePeopleSearch.com

### Description
FreePeopleSearch.com is a public records search engine that provides free access to detailed personal information about individuals in the United States. The service allows users to look up people and retrieve data including addresses, phone numbers, arrest records, court records, marriage and divorce records, and lists of relatives. Because this comprehensive information is aggregated and made available at no cost, it poses significant privacy risks to individuals. The ease of access to sensitive data such as location history and legal records can facilitate malicious activities like stalking, doxxing, identity theft, and harassment. Bad actors can exploit this freely available information to target people for scams or other harmful purposes. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about the personal information they share online and can request to have their profiles removed from the site's database through its opt-out process.

## FullEnrich

### Description
FullEnrich is a data enrichment platform specializing in providing B2B contact information for sales and marketing professionals. The service utilizes a "waterfall enrichment" technique, aggregating data from over 20 premium vendors to find and verify business leads' email addresses and phone numbers. Its primary customers are B2B companies looking to enhance their outreach efforts by enriching their lead lists with detailed contact and company profiles, including direct emails, mobile numbers, job titles, and social media profiles. This aggregation from numerous sources allows them to claim a higher success rate in finding contact details than single-source providers. The exposure of direct contact information like mobile numbers and personal email addresses poses significant privacy risks. This data can be exploited by malicious actors for targeted phishing campaigns, sophisticated social engineering attacks, or business email compromise fraud. Having such accessible professional data increases the risk of unwanted and potentially harassing communications directed at individuals in their workplace. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be mindful of the professional information they share publicly on networking sites and corporate websites. It is also advisable to actively seek out and request removal from data broker platforms like FullEnrich to reduce their digital footprint.

### Description

The service is primarily used by organizations for researching and tracking information on companies, markets, investment funds, and key personnel. Golden's platform aggregates fragmented web data into structured profiles that include details like funding history, leadership changes, and growth metrics, which clients can access to identify high-growth companies and track executive moves. While focused on business data, the inclusion of information about executives and other professionals poses privacy risks, as this data could be exploited for targeted phishing, social engineering, or other business-related scams. To mitigate such risks, individuals should be cautious about the professional information they share publicly and can request to have their data removed from the platform by contacting the company.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://golden.com/home](https://golden.com/home)
- **Email**: hello@golden-support.com
- **Type**: B2B Lead Generation
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

## GovQA

### Description
GovQA, a subsidiary of Granicus, provides a software platform primarily used by government agencies to manage and respond to public records requests, such as those filed under the Freedom of Information Act (FOIA). The service is not a public-facing database but rather a workflow and compliance tool for cities, counties, and state agencies to handle the intake, processing, and delivery of government records. While GovQA itself does not aggregate and sell data, it facilitates access to public records which can contain a vast amount of personal and sensitive information, including names, addresses, legal records, and more. The primary risk to individuals is the potential exposure of their personal information contained within these government files, which could be misused for identity theft, doxxing, or harassment if not properly redacted or secured by the managing agency. Individuals can best protect themselves by being mindful of the information they provide to government entities and by using the established legal processes, often facilitated by tools like GovQA, to request and review their own records.

## Healthline Media

### Description
Healthline.com is a digital publisher of health and wellness information, offering articles, news, and resources on a wide range of medical conditions and lifestyle topics. The company generates revenue through advertising, sponsored content, and affiliate programs, targeting consumers with health-related information. While not a traditional data broker, Healthline collects significant personal and sensitive data based on users' browsing activity, including the articles they read about specific health conditions. This practice poses privacy risks, as browsing data, including visits to pages on sensitive topics like HIV or depression, has been shared with third-party advertisers and data brokers for targeted advertising. This can lead to users being profiled based on their health interests and receiving highly specific pharmaceutical ads without their direct consent. To protect their privacy, individuals should be mindful of their browsing activity, utilize privacy settings on the site, and use tools like the Global Privacy Control signal, which Healthline is now required to honor.

## HireRight, LLC

### Description
HireRight is a global company that provides employment screening and background check services to businesses. Its primary customers are employers, ranging from small businesses to nearly half of the Fortune 100, who use the service to vet job candidates and current employees. The company creates detailed reports by verifying a candidate's employment and education history, searching criminal records, examining credit history, and conducting drug screenings. HireRight compiles this sensitive data by contacting former employers and educational institutions and accessing public records. The collection of such comprehensive personal information poses significant privacy risks; errors in a report, such as outdated or mixed records, could unjustly cost an individual a job offer and damage their professional reputation. To protect themselves, individuals should be cautious about the information shared on applications and are entitled under laws like the Fair Credit Reporting Act (FCRA) to review their reports and dispute any inaccuracies they find.

Primary customers include businesses across various industries, such as e-commerce, ad tech, and cybersecurity, who use the service to prevent chargebacks, account takeovers, fake account creation, and click fraud. <a id='27254'></a>
## Identiq

### Description
Identiq operates a private peer-to-peer network that enables large companies to collaborate and validate consumer identities for the purpose of fraud prevention. The service is used by businesses in sectors like e-commerce, banking, and fintech to verify new users and transactions without directly sharing any sensitive personal data with each other. Using proprietary cryptographic technology, member companies can confirm whether a user is trusted by others on the network, reducing friction for legitimate customers while blocking bad actors. While this model is designed to enhance privacy by not exposing raw personal information, it still involves creating a trust profile of individuals based on their collective activity across different services. The primary risk for individuals is not public data exposure, but the potential for being algorithmically denied services based on a negative validation within this closed network, which could result from inaccurate data. To protect themselves, individuals should be cautious about the information they share with online services and can exercise their data rights by contacting the companies they do business with directly.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://identiqs.com](https://identiqs.com)
- **Type**: Profile Data Broker
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

Illinois Prison Talk provides a publicly accessible database of individuals incarcerated within the Illinois prison system. The website allows users to search for inmates and view details such as their name, inmate number, current correctional facility, and sentencing information. This service aggregates public records related to inmate populations, making them easily searchable for anyone, including family members, friends, and the general public. The accessibility of this sensitive information poses significant privacy risks. Exposing details about an individual's incarceration can lead to harassment, stalking, and social stigma for both the inmates and their families. This data could be exploited by malicious actors for targeted scams, identity theft, or doxxing, creating a difficult environment for rehabilitation and reintegration into society. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about the personal information they share online and can explore options to have their data removed from such public-facing databases.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://illinoisprisontalk.org/](https://illinoisprisontalk.org/)
- **Opt-Out URL**: [https://illinoisprisontalk.org/remove-my-info.php](https://illinoisprisontalk.org/remove-my-info.php)
- **Type**: People Search Site
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

## JailBase

### Description
JailBase is an online platform that provides public access to arrest records and mugshots from various county and jurisdiction jail systems across the United States. The service aggregates and publishes inmate data, including booking information and charges, making it searchable for free. Their database contains millions of arrest records, with new information added daily. The primary users of JailBase are members of the public, legal professionals, and journalists seeking up-to-date incarceration data. The platform's notable features include a searchable database of recent arrests and the ability to receive notifications if someone you know gets arrested. The exposure of such sensitive information, including mugshots and arrest details, poses significant privacy risks, as this data can be easily accessed and potentially misused for harassment, doxxing, or public shaming, even if the individual is not convicted of a crime. <a id='26279'></a>
## LENSO AI SPÓŁKA AKCYJNA

### Description
Lenso.ai is an advanced reverse image search engine that utilizes artificial intelligence and facial recognition to find where photos appear online across billions of images. Users can upload an image to search for people, places, and duplicate or similar content, making it a powerful tool for tracking one's own digital footprint. The platform's core feature is its facial recognition search, which allows anyone to upload a photo of a person and discover where else that individual's face appears on the public internet. This capability presents significant privacy risks, as it can be used to identify, track, and gather information on individuals without their consent, potentially leading to stalking, doxxing, and harassment. Bad actors could misuse this technology to compile dossiers on people, uncover private information, or identify anonymous individuals from a single photograph. To protect their privacy, individuals should be cautious about the images they share online and can request to have their images removed from Lenso.ai's index through an opt-out form on their website.

<a id='26415'></a>
## LIS Cross-National Data Center in Luxembourg

### Description
LIS, formerly known as The Luxembourg Income Study, is a data archive and research center that provides access to harmonized microdata from numerous high- and middle-income countries for the purposes of socio-economic research. Its primary users are researchers, educators, and policymakers who analyze anonymized data on income, wealth, employment, and demographics to study inequality and social outcomes. The organization houses the Luxembourg Income Study (LIS) Database and the Luxembourg Wealth Study (LWS) Database, which together represent the largest available income database of its kind. While LIS is not a commercial data broker in the typical sense, it manages vast amounts of sensitive personal data, making data protection a critical concern. The main privacy risk associated with such a large collection of microdata is the potential for re-identification of individuals, even though the data is anonymized. To mitigate this, LIS provides access to the data through a secure remote-execution system called LISSY, which prevents researchers from directly downloading the raw data. This controlled environment is designed to protect the privacy of the survey respondents. Individuals can protect themselves by being mindful of the information they share in surveys and by understanding how research institutions use their data.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://lisproject.org/](https://lisproject.org/)
- **Email**: admin@lisdatacenter.org
- **Type**: Profile Data Broker
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

---

<a id='26635'></a>
## Ladders, Inc.

### Description
The Ladders is a prominent online job search platform in the United States that specifically caters to high-earning professionals seeking positions with salaries of $100,000 or more. The service allows individuals to create detailed professional profiles, upload resumes containing their work history, skills, and salary expectations, and apply for vetted, high-paying job opportunities. Its primary customers are both job seekers looking for executive-level roles and recruiters or employers aiming to fill those positions by searching the platform's database of qualified candidates. The exposure of detailed career information, including resumes and salary data, poses privacy risks such as a current employer discovering an employee's job search activities or personal contact information being shared with numerous recruiters. This concentration of high-earner data could also be a target for bad actors seeking to commit sophisticated fraud or identity theft. Individuals can protect themselves by carefully managing the information they choose to share on their public profiles and by reviewing the platform's privacy settings to control data visibility.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://www.theladders.com/](https://www.theladders.com/)
- **Email**: support@theladders.com
- **Type**: Profile Data Broker
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

<a id='26650'></a>
## LawLink

### Description
LawLink.com is an online social and business networking platform designed for attorneys, law students, and other legal professionals. Founded in 2007, the site functions as a large directory, featuring over one million attorney profiles that potential clients can search to find legal representation. Professionals can create public profiles, which are optimized for search engines, and share legal documents like articles, motions, and pleadings to showcase their expertise. While the platform is a tool for professional visibility, the public nature of these profiles means that attorneys' professional information is readily accessible. This exposure could potentially be misused by bad actors for sophisticated phishing schemes, identity misrepresentation, or targeted harassment. To mitigate these risks, legal professionals using the service should be selective about the information they share on their public profiles and regularly review their settings to ensure their privacy.

### Information

### Description
Lawyers.com is an online directory that connects individuals and businesses with legal professionals across the United States. Part of the Martindale-Avvo network, the platform features profiles of attorneys and law firms, allowing users to search for legal assistance by location and area of practice. The information provided on lawyers, such as their professional biographies, work history, and contact details, is primarily sourced from the legal professionals themselves who create and manage their own profiles. While the site serves as a B2B lead generation tool for attorneys, the public display of their professional information could potentially be misused for marketing purposes or unsolicited contact. To mitigate privacy risks, legal professionals should be mindful of the amount of personal information they share publicly and can manage their profile information directly on the site.

<a id='27257'></a>
## LeadAR

### Description
LeadAR is an all-in-one marketing and sales automation platform designed specifically for aesthetic medical practices. The service provides tools for lead capture and nurturing, including email and SMS marketing campaigns, AI-powered chatbots, and reputation management. Their primary customers are aesthetic clinics, and the platform is built to integrate seamlessly with the Aesthetic Record EMR (Electronic Medical Record) system to manage the entire patient journey from initial inquiry to post-treatment follow-up. This deep integration within the aesthetics industry makes it a specialized tool for patient acquisition and retention. The platform handles personal information provided by potential and existing patients of the clinics it serves, which can include names, contact details, and communication history. The primary privacy risk stems from the aggregation of this sensitive patient lead data within a single platform; a data breach could expose individuals' interest in specific aesthetic treatments, leading to potential embarrassment, discrimination, or targeted scams. To protect their information, individuals should be mindful of the data they share when inquiring about services with clinics using such platforms and can exercise their data rights by contacting the clinic directly. It is also crucial to limit the sharing of personal information online and to be aware that opting out would likely need to be handled through the specific aesthetic practice that uses the LeadAR software.

## LocateFamily.com

### Description
LocateFamily.com is a people-search website that publishes personal information, including full names, addresses, and phone numbers, often without the subjects' knowledge. The site claims to help users find lost family and friends by aggregating data from various global sources such as public records, social media, and online forums. The information is freely and publicly accessible, posing significant privacy risks to individuals whose data is exposed. The availability of this sensitive information can be exploited by malicious actors for purposes of stalking, doxxing, identity theft, and harassment. The company has faced legal scrutiny, including a substantial fine from the Dutch Data Protection Authority for violations of privacy law. To protect themselves, individuals should be cautious about the personal information they share online and can request to have their data removed from the site, though the process has been criticized as difficult.

<a id='26554'></a>
## Lookify

### Description
Lookify.io is a reverse phone number lookup service that allows users to identify the owner and gather details associated with a phone number in the United States and Canada. The platform provides information such as the owner's full name, address, carrier, and location. Lookify serves both individuals wanting to identify unknown callers and businesses seeking to verify contacts or generate leads. A notable feature is its "Threat Score," which assesses the likelihood of a number being connected to spam or fraudulent activities based on user reports and other data. By making it easy to connect a phone number to a person's name and physical address, the service poses significant privacy risks, including potential stalking, doxxing, and harassment. Malicious actors could use this readily available information to target individuals for scams or identity theft. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about sharing their phone number publicly and can request the removal of their information from Lookify's database via their opt-out process.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://lookify.io/](https://lookify.io/)
- **Email**: privacy@lookify.io
- **Type**: Phone Directory
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

## MansionQuest.com

### Description
MansionQuest.com, a service provided by Potomac Land Company, specializes in ranking and publishing information on Florida's most expensive residential properties. The site compiles data from the official Property Appraisers in all 67 Florida counties to create lists such as the "TOP 1,000 Houses in Florida," detailing the property's value, its address, and the owner's name. This information is presented as a directory for tracking wealth and exclusive homes within the state. By making the names and addresses of wealthy homeowners publicly accessible in easily searchable lists, MansionQuest.com creates significant privacy and security risks. This exposure can make individuals targets for serious crimes, including home invasion, theft, stalking, and financial fraud. To mitigate such risks, individuals should be cautious about the personal information available in public records and can request to have their information removed from such databases.

## MapQuest, Inc.

### Description
MapQuest is a long-standing web mapping service that provides users with driving directions, maps, and the ability to find business locations. As one of the pioneering online mapping services, it allows individuals to search for addresses, points of interest, and plan routes with features like real-time traffic updates. While the service is free and ad-supported, the exposure of location data, search histories, and saved favorite places can present privacy risks. This information, if not properly managed, could potentially be used to infer personal routines and frequent locations, posing risks of stalking or doxxing. To address these concerns, MapQuest has introduced a privacy-focused app, "Private Maps," which aims to provide navigation without tracking or sharing user data. Individuals can protect their privacy by being mindful of the information they save in their accounts, clearing their search history, and using privacy-centric options when available.

## Massachusetts People Records

### Description
Massachusettspeoplerecords.org is a people search website that provides access to public records for individuals within Massachusetts. The service allows users to search for people and view a range of personal information, which may include details such as addresses, phone numbers, and other public record data. By aggregating and presenting this information, the site makes it easy for anyone to find personal details about Massachusetts residents. The availability of such easily accessible personal data creates significant privacy concerns, as it can be exploited for purposes like doxxing, stalking, identity theft, and harassment. Malicious actors could use this information to target individuals or build more comprehensive profiles for fraudulent activities. To mitigate these risks, it is advisable to be cautious about the information shared publicly online and to utilize any available opt-out procedures to have personal data removed from such databases.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://massachusettspeoplerecords.org/](https://massachusettspeoplerecords.org/)
- **Type**: People Search Site
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

## Men Stopping Violence

### Description
Menstoppingviolence.org is a people search website that allows users to access detailed personal information by searching for an individual's name. The site aggregates public records to provide data such as criminal records, judgments, addresses, phone numbers, social media accounts, and relatives. This service operates deceptively under the name of a former non-profit organization, Men Stopping Violence, which focused on preventing violence against women but ceased operations in mid-2024. The current website exploits the defunct organization's name and mission, creating a misleading impression that could lure in users under false pretenses. Exposing sensitive personal information on a platform with this name poses severe risks, ironically creating a tool that could be used by abusers, stalkers, and other malicious actors to locate and harass individuals, including survivors of violence. To protect one's privacy, it is advisable to limit the amount of personal information shared publicly and to actively seek removal from such databases, though some users have reported that the site's opt-out function is ineffective.

### Description
These days, it seems like everything is moving online. There are many advantages to this digital age, but there are also some disadvantages – especially when it comes to our personal data. One of the biggest problems with websites like MineralHolders is they often collect and store our personal data without our knowledge or consent. These companies are known as data brokers, and their business is buying and selling our personal information. MineralHolders collects and sells information about mineral rights holders – their personal address and location, and their assets and the asset value. This may not seem like a big deal at first glance, but there are actually several disadvantages to having your information on a site like MineralHolders. Here are just a few: If the website is hacked or someone gains unauthorized access to the site, your information could be compromised. Data brokers often sell or trade user data, which means your information could be bought and sold without your knowledge or consent. Data brokers may not have security measures in place to protect your information from theft or misuse. If you are concerned about your online privacy, Optery helps you scan and remove your exposed private information. We cover more than 200 sites and other websites where you can find your personal information exposed. You can sign up for a free Exposure Scan and tools you can use to remove your information, or you can upgrade to one of our paid subscriptions and let our Opt Out Agents help you with the removals. If you’re not comfortable with having your personal information stored on a data broker website like MineralHolders, you can always opt out. To do so, simply go to the website and look for the opt-out link, or, you can follow our step-by-step guide below.

<a id='26412'></a>
## NPIR.org

### Description
NPIR.org serves as a public directory of healthcare providers, specifically those registered within the National Plan & Provider Enumeration System (NPPES). The site provides access to the NPI Registry, a database where every registered healthcare provider is issued a unique National Provider Identifier (NPI) number. This 10-digit identifier is used for standard healthcare transactions, such as submitting insurance claims. The primary users of this service are other healthcare providers, health plans, and clearinghouses who need to verify NPI numbers for administrative and financial purposes as required by HIPAA. While this information is publicly accessible for legitimate healthcare administration, its availability can pose privacy risks. The data exposed includes providers' names, specialties, and practice addresses. This information could potentially be misused by individuals for solicitation, marketing, or to create fraudulent communications targeting healthcare professionals. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about unsolicited contact and can review their data protection rights, which may include requesting erasure of personal data under certain conditions.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://npir.org/](https://npir.org/)
- **Opt-Out URL**: [https://npir.org/privacy](https://npir.org/privacy)
- **Type**: Business Search
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

---

<a id='26636'></a>
## Names and Facts

### Description
Names and Facts is a people search engine that provides public records and personal information for individuals in the United States and Canada. The site allows users to search for people by name to access a wide range of data, including contact details, residence history, criminal records, financial information such as salaries and assets, and details about marriages and divorces. The platform also aggregates information from social networks and dating profiles. The availability of such comprehensive personal data poses significant privacy risks, as it can be exploited for stalking, identity theft, doxxing, and harassment. Bad actors can easily compile detailed profiles on individuals, which can be used for fraudulent activities. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about the amount of personal information they share online and can request to have their information removed from the site's database through their opt-out process.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://namesandfacts.com/](https://namesandfacts.com/)
- **Email**: support@namesandfacts.com
- **Type**: People Search Site
- **Optery Support Tier**: [Custom Removals](https://www.optery.com/pricing)

## NeighborWho

### Description
NeighborWho is a data broker that falls under the umbrella of Beenverified. They are focused on reverse home address lookups. You just input a name or address to conduct a search and NeighborWho returns information about people and properties through the use of a searchable database. Neighborwho posts personal information about the location, the owners, the neighbors, and other property details. This information may have legitimate uses, however, not everyone is comfortable having their personal details exposed online. In fact, exposed data online often leads to spam calls and unwanted emails. In the worst cases, this exposed private information can be a source of phishing attempts, identity theft, and other possible cybercrimes.

### Information

## Nestfully, LLC

### Description
Nestfully.com is a public real estate portal that provides homebuyers and sellers with property listings sourced directly from Multiple Listing Services (MLS). A joint venture between prominent MLS organizations like Bright MLS and California Regional Multiple Listing Service (CRMLS), it aims to provide accurate, ad-free listing information to consumers while connecting them directly with real estate agents at no cost. The platform's primary customers are homebuyers, sellers, and real estate professionals who use it to search for properties and connect with agents. While not a traditional people search site, the service collects personal and sensitive information, including location data, financial details, and internet activity, which it may share with third parties for marketing purposes. This collection of data for real estate transactions and marketing could expose individuals to targeted advertising and potentially unwanted solicitations. To protect their privacy, individuals should be cautious about the information they share and can exercise their data rights through the contact information provided in the site's privacy policy.

## New Work SE

### Description
XING, operated by New Work SE, is a prominent professional networking platform primarily focused on the German-speaking market, including Germany, Austria, and Switzerland, with a user base of over 21 million members. Similar to LinkedIn, the service is designed to connect professionals across various industries, facilitate job searches, and enable companies to recruit talent. Users create detailed professional profiles that include their work history, educational background, skills, and a profile picture, which are then visible to other members and recruiters on the platform. While not a traditional data broker, the platform exposes a significant amount of personal and professional data, which can lead to unsolicited contact from recruiters and other professionals. The concentration of professional data also presents a target for data scraping and potential misuse by bad actors for targeted phishing campaigns or corporate espionage. To mitigate these risks, individuals should carefully configure their privacy settings to control who can view their information and be cautious about the details they share publicly on their profiles.

## NoCallerName

### Description
NoCallerName is a reverse phone lookup service that allows users to identify the owner of a phone number. The service provides access to a database of phone numbers primarily for the United States, returning information such as the full name, current address, and carrier details associated with a number. Its customers include individuals curious about unknown callers, as well as business professionals like recruiters and sales teams who use the service to find or verify contact information. The platform operates on a credit-based system, with monthly subscription plans available. Exposing personal information like names and addresses linked to a phone number creates significant privacy risks, including the potential for stalking, doxxing, and harassment. This readily available information can be exploited by malicious actors for various harmful purposes. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about sharing their phone number online and can request to have their information removed from such databases.

### Information
- **Website**: [https://nocallername.com/](https://nocallername.com/)

The service scours the internet, including professional networks and public data sources, to identify and evaluate potential job candidates based on specific criteria provided by a hiring manager. It then engages with these individuals through personalized, multi-channel outreach campaigns. The platform's primary customers are businesses and executive search firms looking to automate the top of their recruiting funnel and reduce manual sourcing time. By aggregating professional data into detailed candidate profiles, Noon AI creates a risk of misuse if accessed by malicious actors for sophisticated phishing schemes, identity fraud, or targeted harassment under the guise of recruitment. Bad actors could potentially use this information to create more convincing phishing attempts or for doxxing purposes. ## Numbercom

### Description
Numbercom operates as an online platform that virtualizes your mobile phone number, allowing you to use it for various communication services directly from a web browser. The service provides free messaging, chat, and file sharing, with plans to introduce voice and video capabilities, essentially moving mobile communication to an internet-based system while retaining the phone number as the user's identity. By linking your real phone number to this online service, you are entrusting it with your contact point and a key part of your personal identity. This creates potential privacy risks; if the platform is breached or the data is misused, your personal phone number could be exposed and linked to your online activities, increasing the danger of phishing, spam, and social engineering attacks. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about the personal information they share through the platform. It is also wise to limit the personal data shared publicly online and to remove your information from any services you no longer use.

Unlike many social media platforms, it provides lifetime access to its services, such as messaging other members and participating in online reunions, for a one-time membership fee. The platform's primary function is to display names and school affiliations, which can expose personal information that individuals may prefer to keep private. ## OpenCorporates Ltd

### Description
OpenCorporates aggregates and publishes public records for over 200 million corporate entities across 140 jurisdictions, creating the largest open database of company information in the world. The service is utilized by journalists, financial analysts, and compliance professionals for activities like due diligence and investigative reporting. It collects official data including company names, registered addresses, dates of incorporation, and the names of directors. While this information is sourced from public government registries, its consolidation in a single, easily searchable database poses privacy risks to business owners and directors. Personal details, such as names and addresses associated with a company, become readily accessible, which could be misused for doxxing, harassment, or identity theft. Individuals can mitigate these risks by using a registered agent's address instead of a personal one for company filings. Although the data is from public sources, one can request to have their information removed from the platform.

<a id='26557'></a>
## Panjiva, Inc.

### Description
Panjiva, a subsidiary of S&P Global, is a global trade data company that provides intelligence on international supply chains. The subscription-based platform offers access to billions of import and export shipment records from millions of companies worldwide, allowing users to search for suppliers, track competitors, and analyze global trade trends. Their primary customers include importers, exporters, supply chain professionals, and sales and marketing teams who use the data for lead generation, risk analysis, and market research. Panjiva's data is sourced from customs agencies and other commercial sources, which it then aggregates and cleans using machine-learning technologies. While the platform focuses on business-to-business data, the detailed shipping manifests can expose sensitive commercial information, such as supplier and customer relationships, shipment volumes, and product types. This transparency poses a risk of competitive intelligence exploitation, where rivals could use this information to identify a company's suppliers and disrupt their supply chain. Businesses concerned about this exposure can take steps to obscure their exporter details in shipping documents.

## ParcelLookup.com

### Description
Parcellookup.com is a domain used by various county assessor offices throughout the United States to provide public access to property parcel information. It is not a single company but rather a common web address for different local government entities that allow users to search for property data within their specific jurisdiction. These portals typically allow searches by owner name, address, or parcel number, revealing details such as property ownership, assessed value, sales history, and physical characteristics of the property. While this information is a matter of public record, its easy accessibility online can pose privacy risks. The availability of property ownership details linked to names and addresses can be exploited by individuals for purposes of doxxing, stalking, or targeted harassment. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be aware of what information is publicly available about them and can typically contact the specific county assessor's office to inquire about any options for redacting personal information from online databases.

## PhoneCheck Pro

### Description
PhoneCheck Pro functions as a reverse phone lookup directory, enabling users to search for information linked to a specific phone number. Such services typically compile data from various sources to provide details about the phone number's owner, which can include their full name, current and past addresses, and other associated public records. The easy accessibility of this personal information creates significant privacy concerns, as it can be exploited for malicious activities like doxxing, stalking, or identity theft. Unsolicited contact and harassment are also potential risks when personal details are readily available through a simple phone number search. To safeguard personal information, individuals should be mindful of what they share publicly online and can request to have their data removed from such directories.

### Information

## Point Digital Finance, Inc.

### Description
Point Digital Finance, Inc. is a financial technology company that provides homeowners with alternatives to traditional home equity loans, such as Home Equity Investments (HEIs) and Home Equity Lines of Credit (HELOCs). The company gathers extensive personal and financial information directly from applicants, including names, addresses, phone numbers, and home valuation estimates, to prequalify them for its products. To assess risk and finalize these financial agreements, Point also collects data from other sources like credit bureaus and public records, creating detailed profiles of individuals' financial situations and creditworthiness. While not a conventional people search site, the aggregation of highly sensitive financial and personal data presents considerable privacy risks. This information, which can include Social Security numbers, account balances, payment history, and credit scores, is a prime target for identity thieves and fraudsters. Should a data breach occur, this detailed financial information could be exploited to open fraudulent accounts, commit financial theft, or facilitate targeted phishing scams. To mitigate these risks, individuals should be cautious about the information they share online and can review Point's privacy policy to understand how their data is used and shared.
